\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a65a176508b404f80e5f5abd31456712e}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a65a176508b404f80e5f5abd31456712e} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!blend\_poisson\_bf@{blend\_poisson\_bf}}
\index{blend\_poisson\_bf@{blend\_poisson\_bf}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{blend\_poisson\_bf()}{blend\_poisson\_bf()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::blend\+\_\+poisson\+\_\+bf (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{array1,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{array2,  }\item[{const int}]{iterations = {\ttfamily 500},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Blends two arrays using Poisson blending with a brute-\/force solver. 

This function performs Poisson blending between {\ttfamily array1} and {\ttfamily array2} over a specified number of iterations. Optionally, a mask can be provided to control the blending regions.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em array1} & The first input array. \\
\hline
{\em array2} & The second input array. \\
\hline
{\em iterations} & The number of iterations for the blending process (default\+: 500). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+mask} & Optional pointer to an array defining the blending mask. If null, blending is applied globally. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The blended array resulting from the Poisson blending operation.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!deposition\_fill\_holes@{deposition\_fill\_holes}}
\index{deposition\_fill\_holes@{deposition\_fill\_holes}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{deposition\_fill\_holes()}{deposition\_fill\_holes()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::deposition\+\_\+fill\+\_\+holes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{int}]{deposition\+\_\+ir,  }\item[{float}]{deposition\+\_\+strength,  }\item[{int}]{iterations = {\ttfamily 1} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Fill holes using Gaussian-\/based deposition. 

Applies a smoothing/deposition pass that fills local depressions while preserving overall terrain shape through gradient-\/aware blending.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Heightmap to modify (in-\/place). \\
\hline
{\em deposition\+\_\+ir} & Influence radius of the Gaussian filter. \\
\hline
{\em deposition\+\_\+strength} & Blending factor controlling deposition intensity. \\
\hline
{\em iterations} & Number of successive deposition passes. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{hydraulic\_particle()}{hydraulic\_particle()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::hydraulic\+\_\+particle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{int}]{nparticles,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+bedrock = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+moisture\+\_\+map = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+elevation\+\_\+shift = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+erosion\+\_\+map = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{float}]{c\+\_\+capacity = {\ttfamily 10.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{c\+\_\+erosion = {\ttfamily 0.05\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{c\+\_\+deposition = {\ttfamily 0.05\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{c\+\_\+inertia = {\ttfamily 0.1\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{c\+\_\+gravity = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{drag\+\_\+rate = {\ttfamily 0.001\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{evap\+\_\+rate = {\ttfamily 0.001\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{enable\+\_\+directional\+\_\+bias = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{float}]{angle\+\_\+bias = {\ttfamily 30.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Simulates hydraulic erosion on a heightmap using particle-\/based flow. 

Particles traverse the heightmap {\ttfamily z}, eroding and depositing material according to local slope, capacity, inertia, and optional directional bias.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Heightmap array to modify. \\
\hline
{\em nparticles} & Number of erosion particles to simulate. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed for particle initialization. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+bedrock} & Optional bedrock array to limit erosion. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+moisture\+\_\+map} & Optional moisture map affecting erosion/deposition. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+elevation\+\_\+shift} & Optional elevation shift map. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+erosion\+\_\+map} & Optional output array recording total erosion. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map} & Optional output array recording deposition. \\
\hline
{\em c\+\_\+capacity} & Sediment capacity of each particle. \\
\hline
{\em c\+\_\+erosion} & Erosion rate coefficient. \\
\hline
{\em c\+\_\+deposition} & Deposition rate coefficient. \\
\hline
{\em c\+\_\+inertia} & \doxylink{structhmap_1_1Particle}{Particle} inertia factor. \\
\hline
{\em c\+\_\+gravity} & Gravity effect on particle movement. \\
\hline
{\em drag\+\_\+rate} & \doxylink{structhmap_1_1Particle}{Particle} velocity damping. \\
\hline
{\em evap\+\_\+rate} & Sediment evaporation rate. \\
\hline
{\em enable\+\_\+directional\+\_\+bias} & Enable bias along a preferred slope direction. \\
\hline
{\em angle\+\_\+bias} & Bias angle in degrees (if directional bias enabled).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{hydraulic\_procedural()}{hydraulic\_procedural()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::hydraulic\+\_\+procedural (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{float}]{kp\+\_\+global,  }\item[{float}]{deposition\+\_\+strength = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{enable\+\_\+default\+\_\+noise = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{noise\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.01\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+kp\+\_\+multiplier = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+angle\+\_\+shift = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ridge\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Apply phase-\/guided hydraulic procedural erosion to a heightmap. 

Computes a phase field from the input terrain and generates ridge-\/aligned erosion patterns modulated by flow accumulation and local gradient. Optionally applies procedural noise, deposition, and outputs a ridge mask.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em z} & Heightmap to erode (modified in place). \\
\hline
 & {\em kp\+\_\+global} & Global kernel size controlling feature scale. \\
\hline
 & {\em c\+\_\+erosion} & Global erosion intensity. \\
\hline
 & {\em seed} & Random seed for phase/noise generation. \\
\hline
 & {\em erosion\+\_\+profile} & Ridge shaping profile type. \\
\hline
 & {\em erosion\+\_\+profile\+\_\+parameter} & Parameter controlling the profile shape. \\
\hline
 & {\em angle\+\_\+shift} & Global phase angle offset (degrees). \\
\hline
 & {\em phase\+\_\+smoothing} & Controls smoothing between phase transitions. \\
\hline
 & {\em talus\+\_\+ref} & Reference talus angle for flow accumulation. \\
\hline
 & {\em gradient\+\_\+scaling\+\_\+ratio} & Blend factor for gradient-\/based modulation. \\
\hline
 & {\em gradient\+\_\+power} & Exponent applied to normalized gradient. \\
\hline
 & {\em apply\+\_\+deposition} & If true, applies post-\/erosion deposition pass. \\
\hline
 & {\em enable\+\_\+default\+\_\+noise} & If true, generates internal FBM noise fields. \\
\hline
 & {\em noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of procedural noise. \\
\hline
 & {\em p\+\_\+kp\+\_\+multiplier} & Optional spatial modulation of kernel size. \\
\hline
 & {\em p\+\_\+angle\+\_\+shift} & Optional spatial phase shift. \\
\hline
 & {\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional external noise field (x component). \\
\hline
 & {\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional external noise field (y component). \\
\hline
 & {\em p\+\_\+ridge\+\_\+mask} & Optional output ridge mask (cosine of phase). \\
\hline
 & {\em bbox} & World-\/space bounding box.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Multi-\/octave (f\+Bm) variant of \doxylink{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_afbecd3a8ce025fb08ca3296ce81f695d}{hydraulic\+\_\+procedural()}. 

Applies the erosion operator across multiple octaves with lacunarity/persistence scaling, accumulating a normalized ridge mask.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em z} & Heightmap to erode (modified in place). \\
\hline
 & {\em kp\+\_\+global} & Base kernel size. \\
\hline
 & {\em c\+\_\+erosion} & Base erosion intensity. \\
\hline
 & {\em seed} & Random seed. \\
\hline
 & {\em erosion\+\_\+profile} & Ridge shaping profile. \\
\hline
 & {\em octaves} & Number of f\+Bm octaves. \\
\hline
 & {\em persistence} & Amplitude decay per octave. \\
\hline
 & {\em lacunarity} & Frequency growth per octave. \\
\hline
 & {\em erosion\+\_\+profile\+\_\+parameter} & Profile parameter. \\
\hline
 & {\em angle\+\_\+shift} & Global phase shift (degrees). \\
\hline
 & {\em phase\+\_\+smoothing} & Phase smoothing factor. \\
\hline
 & {\em talus\+\_\+ref} & Reference talus angle. \\
\hline
 & {\em gradient\+\_\+scaling\+\_\+ratio} & Gradient modulation ratio. \\
\hline
 & {\em gradient\+\_\+power} & Gradient exponent. \\
\hline
 & {\em apply\+\_\+deposition} & Enable deposition pass. \\
\hline
 & {\em enable\+\_\+default\+\_\+noise} & Enable internal noise generation. \\
\hline
 & {\em noise\+\_\+amp} & Noise amplitude. \\
\hline
 & {\em p\+\_\+kp\+\_\+multiplier} & Optional spatial kernel modulation. \\
\hline
 & {\em p\+\_\+angle\+\_\+shift} & Optional spatial phase shift. \\
\hline
 & {\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional external noise (x). \\
\hline
 & {\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional external noise (y). \\
\hline
 & {\em p\+\_\+ridge\+\_\+mask} & Optional accumulated ridge mask output. \\
\hline
 & {\em bbox} & World-\/space bounding box.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{hydraulic\_schott()}{hydraulic\_schott()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::hydraulic\+\_\+schott (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{int}]{iterations,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{talus,  }\item[{float}]{c\+\_\+erosion = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{c\+\_\+thermal = {\ttfamily 0.1\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{c\+\_\+deposition = {\ttfamily 0.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{flow\+\_\+acc\+\_\+exponent = {\ttfamily 0.8\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{flow\+\_\+acc\+\_\+exponent\+\_\+depo = {\ttfamily 0.8\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{flow\+\_\+routing\+\_\+exponent = {\ttfamily 1.3\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{thermal\+\_\+weight = {\ttfamily 1.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{deposition\+\_\+weight = {\ttfamily 2.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+flow = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Simulates hydraulic erosion and deposition on a heightmap using the Schott method. 

This function performs hydraulic erosion on the given heightmap {\ttfamily z} over a specified number of iterations. It includes parameters for controlling erosion, deposition, and flow routing. Optional flow accumulation can also be computed and stored in the {\ttfamily p\+\_\+flow} array.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em z} & The heightmap array to be modified. Heights are updated in-\/place. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em iterations} & The number of iterations for the hydraulic erosion process. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em talus} & An array defining the slope threshold for erosion. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em c\+\_\+erosion} & Erosion coefficient (default\+: 1.\+0f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em c\+\_\+thermal} & Thermal erosion coefficient (default\+: 0.\+1f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em c\+\_\+deposition} & Deposition coefficient (default\+: 0.\+2f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em flow\+\_\+acc\+\_\+exponent} & Exponent controlling the influence of flow accumulation on erosion (default\+: 0.\+8f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em flow\+\_\+acc\+\_\+exponent\+\_\+depo} & Exponent controlling the influence of flow accumulation on deposition (default\+: 0.\+8f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em flow\+\_\+routing\+\_\+exponent} & Exponent controlling flow routing behavior (default\+: 1.\+3f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em thermal\+\_\+weight} & Weight of thermal erosion effects (default\+: 1.\+5f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em deposition\+\_\+weight} & Weight of deposition effects (default\+: 2.\+5f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em p\+\_\+flow} & Optional pointer to an array for storing flow accumulation data. If null, flow data is not returned (default\+: nullptr).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Taken from \href{https://hal.science/hal-04565030v1/document}{\texttt{ https\+://hal.\+science/hal-\/04565030v1/document}}

Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!mudslide@{mudslide}}
\index{mudslide@{mudslide}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mudslide()}{mudslide()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::mudslide (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{landslide\+\_\+mask,  }\item[{float}]{depth,  }\item[{int}]{iterations,  }\item[{float}]{depth\+\_\+map\+\_\+exponent = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{viscosity\+\_\+law\+\_\+power = {\ttfamily 1.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+depth\+\_\+end = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+depth\+\_\+init = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Simulate a mudslide (landslide-\/driven material redistribution) on a height field. 

Applies an iterative viscous flow process to the height array {\ttfamily z}, constrained by {\ttfamily landslide\+\_\+mask} and limited by the specified {\ttfamily depth}. The flow behavior is controlled by a depth exponent and a viscosity power law. Optionally outputs the transported depth map.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em z} & Input/output height field modified in place. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em landslide\+\_\+mask} & Mask defining affected areas (non-\/zero = active). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em depth} & Maximum erosion/deposition depth. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em iterations} & Number of simulation iterations. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em depth\+\_\+map\+\_\+exponent} & Exponent applied to depth influence (default 0.\+5f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em viscosity\+\_\+law\+\_\+power} & Power exponent controlling viscosity response (default 1.\+5f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em p\+\_\+depth} & Optional pointer to store resulting depth map (nullable).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rifts()}{rifts()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::rifts (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{const glm\+::vec2 \&}]{kw,  }\item[{float}]{angle,  }\item[{float}]{amplitude,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{elevation\+\_\+noise\+\_\+shift = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smooth\+\_\+bottom = {\ttfamily 0.05\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smooth\+\_\+top = {\ttfamily 0.05\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{radial\+\_\+spread\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{elevation\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.1\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{clamp\+\_\+vmin = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{remap\+\_\+vmin = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{apply\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{bool}]{reverse\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{float}]{mask\+\_\+gamma = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const glm\+::vec2 \&}]{center = {\ttfamily \{0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{const glm\+::vec4 \&}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Applies a "{}rift"{} deformation effect to a heightmap array. 

This function modifies the given heightmap by introducing linear or radial "{}rift-\/like"{} noise patterns. The deformation can be controlled by several parameters such as direction, amplitude, noise shifts, and optional external noise arrays. Optionally, the effect can be masked using a power-\/based blending function.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Reference to the heightmap array to be modified in-\/place. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Frequency vector (kx, ky) scaling the deformation in X and Y directions. \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Orientation of the rift in degrees (0° = horizontal, 90° = vertical). \\
\hline
{\em amplitude} & Strength of the rift deformation applied to the heightmap. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed used for deterministic noise generation. \\
\hline
{\em elevation\+\_\+noise\+\_\+shift} & Vertical offset applied to the base noise to shift elevation influence. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smooth\+\_\+bottom} & Lower smoothing factor for Voronoi-\/based noise computation. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smooth\+\_\+top} & Upper smoothing factor for Voronoi-\/based noise computation. \\
\hline
{\em radial\+\_\+spread\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude controlling radial spreading away from the rift axis. \\
\hline
{\em elevation\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude scaling the influence of the heightmap\textquotesingle{}s initial values as noise input. \\
\hline
{\em clamp\+\_\+vmin} & Minimum clamp value for the Voronoi noise before remapping. \\
\hline
{\em remap\+\_\+vmin} & Minimum remap value for scaling noise output. \\
\hline
{\em apply\+\_\+mask} & If true, applies a power-\/based blending mask instead of a direct overwrite. \\
\hline
{\em mask\+\_\+gamma} & Gamma exponent used when applying the mask to control blending. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to an external noise array for X-\/offset perturbation (nullptr if unused). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to an external noise array for Y-\/offset perturbation (nullptr if unused). \\
\hline
{\em center} & 2D vector specifying the central point around which the rift effect is computed. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box (xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax) defining the spatial domain of the heightmap.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::sediment\+\_\+deposition (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+mask,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{talus,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{float}]{max\+\_\+deposition = {\ttfamily 0.01},  }\item[{int}]{iterations = {\ttfamily 5},  }\item[{int}]{thermal\+\_\+subiterations = {\ttfamily 10} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::sediment\+\_\+deposition (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{talus,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{float}]{max\+\_\+deposition = {\ttfamily 0.01},  }\item[{int}]{iterations = {\ttfamily 5},  }\item[{int}]{thermal\+\_\+subiterations = {\ttfamily 10} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_aec782e6aba3f4cfbbd97aafa46cc700b}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_aec782e6aba3f4cfbbd97aafa46cc700b}

\index{sediment\_layer@{sediment\_layer}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sediment\_layer()}{sediment\_layer()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::sediment\+\_\+layer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{talus\+\_\+layer,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{talus\+\_\+upper\+\_\+limit,  }\item[{int}]{iterations,  }\item[{bool}]{apply\+\_\+post\+\_\+filter = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Applies a talus-\/based sediment deposition layer. 

Computes a sediment (deposition) map using thermal erosion constrained by per-\/cell talus limits. Optionally smooths the result and blends it back into the heightmap.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em z} & Heightmap to modify. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em talus\+\_\+layer} & Base talus values for erosion. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em talus\+\_\+upper\+\_\+limit} & Upper talus threshold used for masking. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em iterations} & Number of erosion iterations. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em apply\+\_\+post\+\_\+filter} & Enable post smoothing and blending. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map} & Optional output deposition map (may be null).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{strata()}{strata()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::strata (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{float}]{angle,  }\item[{float}]{slope,  }\item[{float}]{gamma,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{bool}]{linear\+\_\+gamma = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{kz = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 4},  }\item[{float}]{lacunarity = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{gamma\+\_\+noise\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{noise\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.4\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const glm\+::vec2 \&}]{noise\+\_\+kw = {\ttfamily \{4.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~4.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{bool}]{enable\+\_\+ridge\+\_\+noise = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{const glm\+::vec2 \&}]{ridge\+\_\+noise\+\_\+kw = {\ttfamily \{4.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{float}]{ridge\+\_\+angle\+\_\+shift = {\ttfamily 45.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{ridge\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{ridge\+\_\+clamp\+\_\+vmin = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{ridge\+\_\+remap\+\_\+vmin = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{apply\+\_\+elevation\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{bool}]{apply\+\_\+ridge\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{mask\+\_\+gamma = {\ttfamily 0.4\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const glm\+::vec4 \&}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Applies stratification to a heightfield using directional noise and multiscale gamma transformations. 

This function modifies the input heightfield {\ttfamily z} by simulating geological strata patterns. It combines directional shifts, fractal noise, and ridge-\/based perturbations to produce layered structures in the data. The MUST BE NORMALIZED in \mbox{[}0, 1\mbox{]}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Reference to the heightfield array to modify, MUST BE NORMALIZED in \mbox{[}0, 1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Horizontal orientation of the strata in degrees. \\
\hline
{\em slope} & Vertical slope of the strata. \\
\hline
{\em gamma} & Gamma exponent for the non-\/linear remapping (e.\+g., 0.\+5 for smoothing, 1.\+5 for sharpening). \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Seed for deterministic noise generation. \\
\hline
{\em linear\+\_\+gamma} & If true, applies sharp linear gamma mapping; if false, uses smooth gamma mapping. \\
\hline
{\em kz} & Base scaling factor for the stratification frequency. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of iterative stratification passes (multiscale detail). \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & Frequency multiplier applied at each octave for fractal scaling. \\
\hline
{\em gamma\+\_\+noise\+\_\+ratio} & Ratio controlling how noise influences gamma variation (0 = no noise, 1 = full influence). \\
\hline
{\em noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of the base Perlin noise used to modulate the strata. \\
\hline
{\em noise\+\_\+kw} & Frequency vector for the base Perlin noise along X and Y axes. \\
\hline
{\em ridge\+\_\+noise\+\_\+kw} & Frequency vector for the Voronoi ridge noise (x = main frequency, y = directional frequency). \\
\hline
{\em ridge\+\_\+angle\+\_\+shift} & Additional angular shift (in degrees) for the ridge direction, relative to {\ttfamily angle}. \\
\hline
{\em ridge\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of the ridge noise modulation. \\
\hline
{\em ridge\+\_\+clamp\+\_\+vmin} & Minimum clamp value for ridge noise response. \\
\hline
{\em ridge\+\_\+remap\+\_\+vmin} & Minimum remap value for ridge modulation (used for reverse remapping). \\
\hline
{\em apply\+\_\+mask} & If true, applied an elevation mask on the effect. \\
\hline
{\em mask\+\_\+gamma} & Gamma applied to the mask used for blending original and stratified values for the elevation mask. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+mask} & Optional filter mask, expected in the range \mbox{[}0, 1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box of the domain as {\ttfamily \{xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax\}}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Setting {\ttfamily linear\+\_\+gamma} to {\ttfamily false} produces smoother transitions, while {\ttfamily true} creates sharper layer boundaries.
\item Increasing {\ttfamily octaves} adds multiscale detail but also increases computational cost.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{strata\_cells()}{strata\_cells()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::strata\+\_\+cells (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{float}]{amp,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{gamma = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{gamma\+\_\+lateral = {\ttfamily 0.4\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{angle = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{noise\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{absolute\+\_\+displacement = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{occurence\+\_\+probability = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Applies procedural stratified cell displacement to a heightmap. 

Generates layered cell-\/like structures with optional directional distortion and noise-\/based perturbation.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Heightmap array to modify. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Cell frequency (x,y). \\
\hline
{\em amp} & Displacement amplitude. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed. \\
\hline
{\em gamma} & Vertical shaping exponent. \\
\hline
{\em gamma\+\_\+lateral} & Lateral shaping exponent. \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Layer orientation angle (degrees). \\
\hline
{\em noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of input distortion noise. \\
\hline
{\em absolute\+\_\+displacement} & Use absolute instead of relative displacement. \\
\hline
{\em occurence\+\_\+probability} & Probability of cell activation. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional X distortion field. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional Y distortion field. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Domain bounding box.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{strata\_cells@{strata\_cells}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{strata\_cells()}{strata\_cells()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::strata\+\_\+cells (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{float}]{amp,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+mask,  }\item[{float}]{gamma = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{gamma\+\_\+lateral = {\ttfamily 0.4\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{angle = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{noise\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{absolute\+\_\+displacement = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{occurence\+\_\+probability = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Applies stratified cell displacement with optional masking. 

If {\ttfamily p\+\_\+mask} is provided, the effect is blended with the original heightmap using the mask as interpolation weight.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Heightmap array to modify. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Cell frequency (x,y). \\
\hline
{\em amp} & Displacement amplitude. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+mask} & Optional mask controlling spatial blending. \\
\hline
{\em gamma} & Vertical shaping exponent. \\
\hline
{\em gamma\+\_\+lateral} & Lateral shaping exponent. \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Layer orientation angle (degrees). \\
\hline
{\em noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of input distortion noise. \\
\hline
{\em absolute\+\_\+displacement} & Use absolute instead of relative displacement. \\
\hline
{\em occurence\+\_\+probability} & Probability of cell activation. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional X distortion field. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional Y distortion field. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Domain bounding box.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{strata\_cells\_fbm()}{strata\_cells\_fbm()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::strata\+\_\+cells\+\_\+fbm (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{float}]{amp,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{gamma = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{gamma\+\_\+lateral = {\ttfamily 0.4\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{angle = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{enable\+\_\+default\+\_\+noise = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{default\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.05\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{absolute\+\_\+displacement = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{occurence\+\_\+probability = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{persistence = {\ttfamily 0.4\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{lacunarity = {\ttfamily 2.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Applies multi-\/octave (f\+Bm) stratified cell displacement. 

Accumulates several scaled {\ttfamily strata\+\_\+cells} layers using persistence and lacunarity. Can optionally generate internal distortion noise.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Heightmap array to modify. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Base cell frequency (x,y). \\
\hline
{\em amp} & Base displacement amplitude. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed. \\
\hline
{\em gamma} & Vertical shaping exponent. \\
\hline
{\em gamma\+\_\+lateral} & Lateral shaping exponent. \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Layer orientation angle (degrees). \\
\hline
{\em enable\+\_\+default\+\_\+noise} & Generate internal distortion noise. \\
\hline
{\em default\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of generated noise. \\
\hline
{\em absolute\+\_\+displacement} & Use absolute instead of relative displacement. \\
\hline
{\em occurence\+\_\+probability} & Probability of cell activation. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of f\+Bm layers. \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & Amplitude multiplier per octave. \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & Frequency multiplier per octave. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional X distortion field. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional Y distortion field. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Domain bounding box.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{strata\_cells\_fbm@{strata\_cells\_fbm}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{strata\_cells\_fbm()}{strata\_cells\_fbm()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::strata\+\_\+cells\+\_\+fbm (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{float}]{amp,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+mask,  }\item[{float}]{gamma = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{gamma\+\_\+lateral = {\ttfamily 0.4\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{angle = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{enable\+\_\+default\+\_\+noise = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{default\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.05\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{absolute\+\_\+displacement = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{occurence\+\_\+probability = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{persistence = {\ttfamily 0.4\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{lacunarity = {\ttfamily 2.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Applies masked multi-\/octave stratified cell displacement. 

Works like {\ttfamily strata\+\_\+cells\+\_\+fbm} but blends the result with the original heightmap using {\ttfamily p\+\_\+mask}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Heightmap array to modify. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Base cell frequency (x,y). \\
\hline
{\em amp} & Base displacement amplitude. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+mask} & Optional mask controlling spatial blending. \\
\hline
{\em gamma} & Vertical shaping exponent. \\
\hline
{\em gamma\+\_\+lateral} & Lateral shaping exponent. \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Layer orientation angle (degrees). \\
\hline
{\em enable\+\_\+default\+\_\+noise} & Generate internal distortion noise. \\
\hline
{\em default\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of generated noise. \\
\hline
{\em absolute\+\_\+displacement} & Use absolute instead of relative displacement. \\
\hline
{\em occurence\+\_\+probability} & Probability of cell activation. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of f\+Bm layers. \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & Amplitude multiplier per octave. \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & Frequency multiplier per octave. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional X distortion field. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional Y distortion field. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Domain bounding box.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\bfseries{Result}}  \Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a9ed6ad946ac7bcb852974a38eca78ac8}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a9ed6ad946ac7bcb852974a38eca78ac8} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!strata\_terrace@{strata\_terrace}}
\index{strata\_terrace@{strata\_terrace}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{strata\_terrace()}{strata\_terrace()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::strata\+\_\+terrace (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{float}]{gamma,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{kz = {\ttfamily 4.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{linear\+\_\+gamma = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{gamma\+\_\+noise\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Applies a terrace (stratification) filter to a heightmap. 

Quantizes elevation into kz strata levels and shapes terrace transitions using a gamma profile. Optional noise can modulate the profile.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Heightmap modified in place. \\
\hline
{\em gamma} & Terrace profile exponent (e.\+g. 0.\+5 = sharper, 1.\+5 = smoother). \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed used for profile variation. \\
\hline
{\em kz} & Number of strata levels. \\
\hline
{\em linear\+\_\+gamma} & If true, uses linear terrace transitions. \\
\hline
{\em gamma\+\_\+noise\+\_\+ratio} & Influence of noise on the terrace profile. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise} & Optional noise map for profile modulation.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\DoxyCodeLine{}

{\bfseries{Result}}  \Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_aa75d564b4578a7b56c64cdd8bf740f3e}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_aa75d564b4578a7b56c64cdd8bf740f3e} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!strata\_terrace@{strata\_terrace}}
\index{strata\_terrace@{strata\_terrace}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{strata\_terrace()}{strata\_terrace()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::strata\+\_\+terrace (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{float}]{gamma,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+mask,  }\item[{float}]{kz = {\ttfamily 4.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{linear\+\_\+gamma = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{gamma\+\_\+noise\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Applies a masked terrace (stratification) filter to a heightmap. 

Same as \doxylink{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a9ed6ad946ac7bcb852974a38eca78ac8}{strata\+\_\+terrace()}, but only affects regions defined by p\+\_\+mask.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Heightmap modified in place. \\
\hline
{\em gamma} & Terrace profile exponent. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed used for profile variation. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+mask} & Optional mask controlling where terraces are applied. \\
\hline
{\em kz} & Number of strata levels. \\
\hline
{\em linear\+\_\+gamma} & If true, uses linear terrace transitions. \\
\hline
{\em gamma\+\_\+noise\+\_\+ratio} & Influence of noise on the terrace profile. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise} & Optional noise map for profile modulation.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_ae57a1e9bd94f218d4be17c9d8be012c3}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_ae57a1e9bd94f218d4be17c9d8be012c3} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!thermal\_inflate@{thermal\_inflate}}
\index{thermal\_inflate@{thermal\_inflate}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{thermal\_inflate()}{thermal\_inflate()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::thermal\+\_\+inflate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{talus,  }\item[{int}]{iterations = {\ttfamily 10} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Apply thermal weathering erosion to give a scree like effect. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Input array. \\
\hline
{\em talus} & Talus limit. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map} & \mbox{[}out\mbox{]} Reference to the deposition map, provided as an output field. \\
\hline
{\em iterations} & Number of iterations.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{thermal\_ridge()}{thermal\_ridge()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::thermal\+\_\+ridge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{talus,  }\item[{int}]{iterations = {\ttfamily 10},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Apply thermal weathering erosion to give a ridge like effect. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Based on \href{https://www.fractal-landscapes.co.uk/maths.html}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+fractal-\/landscapes.\+co.\+uk/maths.\+html}}

Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Input array. \\
\hline
{\em talus} & Talus limit. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map} & \mbox{[}out\mbox{]} Reference to the deposition map, provided as an output field. \\
\hline
{\em iterations} & Number of iterations.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_ab753c4abd819aa6945c1cfc5e25ccec4}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_ab753c4abd819aa6945c1cfc5e25ccec4}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{thermal\_scree()}{thermal\_scree()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::thermal\+\_\+scree (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{talus,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{zmax,  }\item[{int}]{iterations = {\ttfamily 10},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs thermal scree erosion on a heightmap. 

This function applies a thermal erosion process that redistributes material from steeper slopes to flatter areas, simulating talus formation. The process iterates a given number of times to achieve a more stable terrain profile.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em z} & The heightmap to be modified in-\/place by the erosion process. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em talus} & The threshold slope angles that determine where material is moved. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em zmax} & The maximum allowed elevation for erosion effects. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em iterations} & The number of erosion iterations to apply (default\+: 10). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map} & Optional pointer to an array that stores the deposited material per cell. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_acfe28321531d2c03721588054da1446a}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_acfe28321531d2c03721588054da1446a}

\index{thermal\_scree@{thermal\_scree}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::valley\+\_\+fill (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{talus,  }\item[{int}]{iterations = {\ttfamily 100},  }\item[{float}]{gamma = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{ratio = {\ttfamily 0.8\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{zmin = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{zmax = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{elevation\+\_\+max\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{preserve\+\_\+elevation\+\_\+range = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Fill valleys using thermal scree deposition and height-\/based blending. 

Applies an erosion-\/based fill to valleys, then blends the result with the original heightmap using a gamma-\/shaped mask derived from elevation.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Heightmap to modify in place. \\
\hline
{\em talus} & Talus angle map controlling scree deposition. \\
\hline
{\em iterations} & Number of erosion iterations. \\
\hline
{\em gamma} & Gamma applied to the height-\/based mixing mask. \\
\hline
{\em ratio} & Blend ratio controlling valley influence. \\
\hline
{\em zmin} & Minimum height for normalization (auto if zmax \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= zmin). \\
\hline
{\em zmax} & Maximum height for normalization (auto if zmax \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= zmin).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{valley\_fill()}{valley\_fill()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::valley\+\_\+fill (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+mask,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{talus,  }\item[{int}]{iterations = {\ttfamily 100},  }\item[{float}]{gamma = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{ratio = {\ttfamily 0.8\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{zmin = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{zmax = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{elevation\+\_\+max\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{preserve\+\_\+elevation\+\_\+range = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a52a653b3b3be84e8ff2330f30a6b5bf3}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a52a653b3b3be84e8ff2330f30a6b5bf3} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!watershed\_ridge@{watershed\_ridge}}
\index{watershed\_ridge@{watershed\_ridge}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{watershed\_ridge()}{watershed\_ridge()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::watershed\+\_\+ridge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{float}]{amplitude = {\ttfamily 0.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{width = {\ttfamily 32.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{edt\+\_\+exponent = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{int}]{prefilter\+\_\+ir = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a0c714c7fa78e9384806de52a5d039f2f}{Flow\+Direction\+Method}}}]{fd\+\_\+method = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a0c714c7fa78e9384806de52a5d039f2fab1d0e0d533e11bd2532fd9e2f1802894}{Flow\+Direction\+Method\+::\+FDM\+\_\+\+D8}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+scaling = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Carves watershed ridges using basin-\/wise distance transforms. 

Drainage basins are computed using D8 flow routing. For each basin, a distance transform to the basin boundary is evaluated and used to lower elevations near watershed divides, forming ridge lines.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Input elevation field. \\
\hline
{\em amplitude} & Ridge carving strength. \\
\hline
{\em ir} & Smoothing. \\
\hline
{\em edt\+\_\+exponent} & Exponent applied to the distance field to control ridge sharpness.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Elevation field with watershed ridges emphasized.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_ad6240ccabf3a0f858698dc0b77ab619e}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_ad6240ccabf3a0f858698dc0b77ab619e} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!bilateral\_filter@{bilateral\_filter}}
\index{bilateral\_filter@{bilateral\_filter}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bilateral\_filter()}{bilateral\_filter()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::bilateral\+\_\+filter (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{array,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{kernel2d,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{kernel1d,  }\item[{float}]{kernel1d\+\_\+value\+\_\+scaling }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Apply a bilateral filter to an array. 

This function performs edge-\/preserving smoothing by combining a spatial kernel (2D) and a value-\/domain kernel (1D). The spatial kernel controls the influence of neighboring samples based on their position, while the value kernel weights samples according to their value difference.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em array} & Input array to be filtered. \\
\hline
{\em kernel2d} & 2D spatial kernel defining neighborhood weights. \\
\hline
{\em kernel1d} & 1D kernel applied in the value domain. \\
\hline
{\em kernel1d\+\_\+value\+\_\+scaling} & Scaling factor applied to value differences before sampling the 1D kernel.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A new array containing the filtered result.
\end{DoxyReturn}
{\bfseries{Example}} 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}


{\bfseries{Result}}  \Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a0cd7116e5c346fe9534e25b53d5e054a}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a0cd7116e5c346fe9534e25b53d5e054a} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!bilateral\_filter@{bilateral\_filter}}
\index{bilateral\_filter@{bilateral\_filter}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bilateral\_filter()}{bilateral\_filter()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::bilateral\+\_\+filter (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{array,  }\item[{int}]{ir,  }\item[{float}]{kernel1d\+\_\+value\+\_\+scaling }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Apply a bilateral filter to an array using a radius-\/based Gaussian kernel. 

This overload builds the spatial kernel implicitly from the given radius. The value-\/domain kernel behavior is controlled by the same scaling factor as the main overload.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em array} & Input array to be filtered. \\
\hline
{\em ir} & Radius of the spatial neighborhood. \\
\hline
{\em kernel1d\+\_\+value\+\_\+scaling} & Scaling factor applied to value differences before computing value-\/domain weights.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A new array containing the filtered result.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a0c8c9b43fbd562b0cc3364c9d85c9433}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a0c8c9b43fbd562b0cc3364c9d85c9433} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!project\_talus\_along\_direction@{project\_talus\_along\_direction}}
\index{project\_talus\_along\_direction@{project\_talus\_along\_direction}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{project\_talus\_along\_direction()}{project\_talus\_along\_direction()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::project\+\_\+talus\+\_\+along\+\_\+direction (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{array,  }\item[{float}]{talus,  }\item[{int}]{direction = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Projects array values along a given direction using talus attenuation. 

Applies a directional propagation (D8 convention) where values decay with distance according to a talus coefficient. The computation is performed on the GPU using an Open\+CL kernel.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em array} & Input 2D array. \\
\hline
{\em talus} & Talus coefficient controlling distance-\/based attenuation. \\
\hline
{\em direction} & Propagation direction (D8 convention, range \mbox{[}0–7\mbox{]}).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A new \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} containing the projected values.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The array is temporarily shifted to non-\/negative values to ensure correctness of Open\+CL atomic operations on floats.
\end{DoxyNote}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a1ac328bd9a69f8737550a131d3f9c516}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a1ac328bd9a69f8737550a131d3f9c516} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!flow\_accumulation\_from\_velocity\_field@{flow\_accumulation\_from\_velocity\_field}}
\index{flow\_accumulation\_from\_velocity\_field@{flow\_accumulation\_from\_velocity\_field}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{flow\_accumulation\_from\_velocity\_field()}{flow\_accumulation\_from\_velocity\_field()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::flow\+\_\+accumulation\+\_\+from\+\_\+velocity\+\_\+field (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{u,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{v,  }\item[{int}]{iterations }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Approximates flow accumulation from a 2D velocity field. 

Advects a scalar accumulation field using an Eulerian transport scheme driven by the velocity components (u, v). Repeated iterations approximate upstream contributing area and highlight flow convergence (thalwegs).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em u} & X-\/component of the flow velocity field. \\
\hline
{\em v} & Y-\/component of the flow velocity field. \\
\hline
{\em iterations} & Number of transport iterations to perform.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Flow accumulation field. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_ab2ccca5e12b451191af1edc97cb86fbf}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_ab2ccca5e12b451191af1edc97cb86fbf} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!flow\_simulation@{flow\_simulation}}
\index{flow\_simulation@{flow\_simulation}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{flow\_simulation()}{flow\_simulation()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::flow\+\_\+simulation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{float}]{water\+\_\+depth,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{depth\+\_\+map,  }\item[{int}]{iterations,  }\item[{float}]{dt = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{flux\+\_\+diffusion = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{flux\+\_\+diffusion\+\_\+strength = {\ttfamily 0.01\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{dry\+\_\+out\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



GPU hydraulic flow simulation using a virtual-\/pipes model; simulates shallow-\/water transport over a height field using iterative flux computation and water transport passes, with optional flux diffusion and post-\/simulation depth clamping to remove thin residual water layers. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Terrain height field. \\
\hline
{\em water\+\_\+height} & Global water scaling factor. \\
\hline
{\em depth\+\_\+map} & Initial relative water distribution. \\
\hline
{\em iterations} & Number of simulation steps. \\
\hline
{\em dt} & Time step size. \\
\hline
{\em flux\+\_\+diffusion} & Enables flux smoothing. \\
\hline
{\em flux\+\_\+diffusion\+\_\+strength} & Strength of flux diffusion. \\
\hline
{\em dry\+\_\+out\+\_\+ratio} & Ratio for removing thin remaining water layers.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} Final simulated water depth map. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a7bed0a401445a2b13d8d37e7a34ea598}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a7bed0a401445a2b13d8d37e7a34ea598} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!snow\_simulation@{snow\_simulation}}
\index{snow\_simulation@{snow\_simulation}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{snow\_simulation()}{snow\_simulation()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::snow\+\_\+simulation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{float}]{snow\+\_\+depth,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{fall\+\_\+map,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{melting\+\_\+map,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{talus,  }\item[{int}]{iterations,  }\item[{float}]{dt = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{fall\+\_\+iterations\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+snow = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+visc = {\ttfamily 0.1\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+melt\+\_\+factor = {\ttfamily 0.8\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+depth\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+depth\+\_\+slope\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{post\+\_\+filter = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{thermal\+\_\+talus\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 0.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Simulate snow accumulation and redistribution over a terrain. 

Models snow fall, depth-\/dependent avalanching (above repose angle) and thermal creep smoothing (below repose angle), with optional melting and post-\/filtering. Snow progressively stabilizes into smooth, rounded forms.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Heightfield of the underlying terrain. \\
\hline
{\em snow\+\_\+depth} & Total amount of snow to deposit. \\
\hline
{\em fall\+\_\+map} & Spatial modulation of snow deposition. \\
\hline
{\em melting\+\_\+map} & Spatial melting factor in \mbox{[}0,1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
{\em talus} & Local repose angle (talus slope). \\
\hline
{\em iterations} & Number of simulation steps. \\
\hline
{\em dt} & Time step. \\
\hline
{\em fall\+\_\+iterations\+\_\+ratio} & Fraction of iterations used for snowfall. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+snow} & Avalanche transport coefficient. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+visc} & Thermal creep (sub-\/repose smoothing) coefficient. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+melt\+\_\+factor} & Global melting strength. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+depth\+\_\+ratio} & Controls snow stiffening with depth. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+depth\+\_\+slope\+\_\+ratio} & Depth influence on repose angle. \\
\hline
{\em post\+\_\+filter} & Apply final smoothing pass if true. \\
\hline
{\em thermal\+\_\+talus\+\_\+ratio} & Controls creep strength relative to talus.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Final snow depth field.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a1dbc83521075f7c0179c7157f292b2b2}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a1dbc83521075f7c0179c7157f292b2b2} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!distance\_transform\_jfa@{distance\_transform\_jfa}}
\index{distance\_transform\_jfa@{distance\_transform\_jfa}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{distance\_transform\_jfa()}{distance\_transform\_jfa()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::distance\+\_\+transform\+\_\+jfa (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{array,  }\item[{bool}]{return\+\_\+squared\+\_\+distance = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return the Euclidean distance transform. 

(Almost) exact transform based on the jump flooding algorithm.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em array} & Input array to be transformed, will be converted into binary\+: 1 wherever input is greater than 0, 0 elsewhere. \\
\hline
{\em return\+\_\+squared\+\_\+distance} & Whether the distance returned is squared or not. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} Reference to the output array.
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::badlands (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{rugosity = {\ttfamily 0.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{angle = {\ttfamily 30.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smoothing = {\ttfamily 0.1\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{base\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a synthetic "{}badlands"{} terrain heightmap. 

This function procedurally creates a 2D elevation field resembling badlands (highly eroded terrain with sharp ridges and valleys). It combines fractal noise (FBM) with a Voronoi-\/based primitive, displaced along a specified orientation.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Output array shape (resolution in x and y). \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Frequency vector controlling the scale of the features. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed used for noise and Voronoi generation. \\
\hline
{\em rugosity} & Controls roughness of the fractal noise (higher = more irregular). \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Orientation angle (degrees) of terrain displacements. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smoothing} & Voronoi smoothing parameter (controls ridge sharpness). \\
\hline
{\em base\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of the base displacement noise. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to external displacement noise field (X-\/axis). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to external displacement noise field (Y-\/axis). \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box of the generation domain in normalized coordinates.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} containing the generated badlands heightmap.
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::basalt\+\_\+field (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{warp\+\_\+kw = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a synthetic procedural terrain resembling basaltic landforms. 

This function creates a multi-\/scale procedural field combining large, medium, and small-\/scale Voronoi-\/based patterns, noise warping, and optional flattening, simulating the morphology of fractured basalt or volcanic terrains. The terrain is constructed using a combination of Voronoi diagrams (via {\ttfamily voronoi\+\_\+fbm}) and fractal noise ({\ttfamily noise\+\_\+fbm}), layered with frequency-\/domain manipulations and amplitude/gain controls at each scale.

The final output is a heightmap represented as an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}}, normalized and composed of\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Large-\/scale cellular patterns with smoothed Voronoi edge distances.
\item Medium and small-\/scale structures introducing finer surface variation.
\item Optional rugosity (fine detail) and flattening to simulate erosion or flow effects.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Output resolution (width x height) of the field. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Base wave numbers (frequency) for the terrain features. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Initial seed used for deterministic random generation. \\
\hline
{\em warp\+\_\+kw} & Frequency of the warping noise that displaces Voronoi positions. \\
\hline
{\em large\+\_\+scale\+\_\+warp\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of displacement for large-\/scale Voronoi warping. \\
\hline
{\em large\+\_\+scale\+\_\+gain} & Gain adjustment applied to the large-\/scale features. \\
\hline
{\em large\+\_\+scale\+\_\+amp} & Final amplitude of the large-\/scale height contribution. \\
\hline
{\em medium\+\_\+scale\+\_\+kw\+\_\+ratio} & Scaling factor for the frequency of the medium-\/scale patterns. \\
\hline
{\em medium\+\_\+scale\+\_\+warp\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of warping for the medium-\/scale displacement. \\
\hline
{\em medium\+\_\+scale\+\_\+gain} & Gain control for medium-\/scale modulation. \\
\hline
{\em medium\+\_\+scale\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of the medium-\/scale heightmap. \\
\hline
{\em small\+\_\+scale\+\_\+kw\+\_\+ratio} & Frequency ratio for small-\/scale details. \\
\hline
{\em small\+\_\+scale\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of small-\/scale pattern contribution. \\
\hline
{\em small\+\_\+scale\+\_\+overlay\+\_\+amp} & Additional overlay strength for repeating the small-\/scale pattern. \\
\hline
{\em rugosity\+\_\+kw\+\_\+ratio} & Frequency ratio for high-\/frequency noise applied as fine roughness. \\
\hline
{\em rugosity\+\_\+amp} & Strength of the rugosity (high-\/frequency modulation). \\
\hline
{\em flatten\+\_\+activate} & Enables or disables the final flattening operation. \\
\hline
{\em flatten\+\_\+kw\+\_\+ratio} & Frequency scaling of the flattening noise field. \\
\hline
{\em flatten\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude control of the flattening operation. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to a noise field used to displace grid coordinates in X. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to a noise field used to displace grid coordinates in Y. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & The 2D bounding box (\{xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax\}) over which the terrain is generated.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A procedurally generated {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} representing the synthetic basalt-\/like terrain field.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This function relies on Open\+CL-\/based kernels via the {\ttfamily gpu\+:\+:} namespace.
\item The returned field is normalized in amplitude but may require rescaling to match specific physical units.
\item Adjusting {\ttfamily seed}, {\ttfamily warp\+\_\+kw}, and the gain/amplitude values can produce a wide variety of terrain features.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
