{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::gabor\+\_\+wave (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{angle,  }\item[{float}]{angle\+\_\+spread\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return an array filled with coherence Gabor noise. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} shape. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Noise wavenumbers \{kx, ky\} for each directions. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed number. \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Base orientation angle for the Gabor wavelets (in radians). Defaults to 0. \\
\hline
{\em angle\+\_\+spread\+\_\+ratio} & Ratio that controls the spread of wave orientations around the base angle. Defaults to 1. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Domain bounding box. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} Fractal noise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Taken from \href{https://www.shadertoy.com/view/clGyWm}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+shadertoy.\+com/view/cl\+Gy\+Wm}}

Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::gabor\+\_\+wave (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{angle = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{angle\+\_\+spread\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::gabor\+\_\+wave\+\_\+fbm (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{angle,  }\item[{float}]{angle\+\_\+spread\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{weight = {\ttfamily 0.7\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{persistence = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{lacunarity = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return an array filled with coherence Gabor noise. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} shape. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Noise wavenumbers \{kx, ky\} for each directions. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed number. \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Base orientation angle for the Gabor wavelets (in radians). Defaults to 0. \\
\hline
{\em angle\+\_\+spread\+\_\+ratio} & Ratio that controls the spread of wave orientations around the base angle. Defaults to 1. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of octaves. \\
\hline
{\em weigth} & Octave weighting. \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & Octave persistence. \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & Defines the wavenumber ratio between each octaves. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & Reference to the control parameter array (acts as a multiplier for the weight parameter). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x,p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Reference to the input noise arrays. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Domain bounding box. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} Fractal noise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Taken from \href{https://www.shadertoy.com/view/clGyWm}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+shadertoy.\+com/view/cl\+Gy\+Wm}}

Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a970d42d8f9305065f89dc019be7ae1cf}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a970d42d8f9305065f89dc019be7ae1cf}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::gavoronoise (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{angle,  }\item[{float}]{amplitude = {\ttfamily }\item[{float}]{slope\+\_\+strength = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{branch\+\_\+strength = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a 2D array using the Gavoro\+Noise algorithm, which is a procedural noise technique for terrain generation and other applications. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Dimensions of the output array. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Wave number vector controlling the noise frequency. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Seed value for random number generation. \\
\hline
{\em amplitude} & Amplitude of the noise. \\
\hline
{\em kw\+\_\+multiplier} & Multiplier for wave numbers in the noise function. \\
\hline
{\em slope\+\_\+strength} & Strength of slope-\/based directional erosion in the noise. \\
\hline
{\em branch\+\_\+strength} & Strength of branch-\/like structures in the generated noise. \\
\hline
{\em z\+\_\+cut\+\_\+min} & Minimum cutoff for Z-\/value in the noise. \\
\hline
{\em z\+\_\+cut\+\_\+max} & Maximum cutoff for Z-\/value in the noise. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of octaves for fractal Brownian motion (f\+Bm). \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & Amplitude scaling factor between noise octaves. \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & Frequency scaling factor between noise octaves. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & Optional array for control parameters, can modify the Z cutoff dynamically. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional array for X-\/axis noise perturbation. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional array for Y-\/axis noise perturbation. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box for mapping grid coordinates to world space.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A 2D array containing the generated Gavoro\+Noise values.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Taken from \href{https://www.shadertoy.com/view/MtGcWh}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+shadertoy.\+com/view/\+Mt\+Gc\+Wh}}

Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}
This function leverages an Open\+CL kernel to compute the Gavoro\+Noise values on the GPU, allowing for efficient large-\/scale generation. The kernel applies a combination of fractal Brownian motion (f\+Bm), directional erosion, and other procedural techniques to generate intricate noise patterns.

The optional {\ttfamily p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param}, {\ttfamily p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x}, and {\ttfamily p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} buffers provide additional flexibility for dynamically adjusting noise parameters and perturbations.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{hemisphere\_field()}{hemisphere\_field()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::hemisphere\+\_\+field (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{rmin = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{density = {\ttfamily 0.1\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{jitter = {\ttfamily \{1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{float}]{shift = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+distance = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+density\+\_\+multiplier = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+size\+\_\+multiplier = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a scalar field representing the signed distance to randomly generated hemispheres. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Resolution of the output field (width, height). \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Scaling factor for field coordinates (world units per pixel). \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed generation. \\
\hline
{\em rmin} & Minimum sphere radius (relative to bbox size). \\
\hline
{\em rmax} & Maximum sphere radius (relative to bbox size). \\
\hline
{\em density} & Fraction of pixels covered by polygons (approximate). \\
\hline
{\em jitter} & Random displacement factor applied to sphere vertices. \\
\hline
{\em shift} & Random position shift applied to sphere center. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional displacement noise field in the X direction (nullptr to disable). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional displacement noise field in the Y direction (nullptr to disable). \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box in normalized coordinates \{xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax\}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} 2D array containing the signed distance field.
\end{DoxyReturn}

0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{uplift\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+water\+\_\+depth = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+inland\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates an island heightmap from a land mask using radial profiles, slope shaping, optional noise, and water attenuation. 

Applies elevation shaping inside the land mask using distance-\/based profiles, slope controls, optional radial and slope noise, and water-\/depth modeling.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em land\+\_\+mask} & Binary mask defining the island shape. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+r} & Optional radial noise field (same size as mask). \\
\hline
{\em apex\+\_\+elevation} & Maximum elevation at island center. \\
\hline
{\em filter\+\_\+distance} & Enable smoothing of the distance transform. \\
\hline
{\em filter\+\_\+ir} & Radius of the distance filter. \\
\hline
{\em slope\+\_\+min} & Minimum slope. \\
\hline
{\em slope\+\_\+max} & Maximum slope. \\
\hline
{\em slope\+\_\+start} & Start of slope ramp (0–1). \\
\hline
{\em slope\+\_\+end} & End of slope ramp (0–1). \\
\hline
{\em slope\+\_\+noise\+\_\+intensity} & Intensity of slope noise modulation. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smooth} & Smoothing factor for the final profile. \\
\hline
{\em radial\+\_\+noise\+\_\+intensity} & Intensity of radial displacement noise. \\
\hline
{\em radial\+\_\+profile\+\_\+gain} & Exponent for radial falloff. \\
\hline
{\em water\+\_\+decay} & Transition sharpness to water level. \\
\hline
{\em water\+\_\+depth} & Water depth below the shoreline. \\
\hline
{\em lee\+\_\+angle} & Angle for lee-\/side (wind shadow) erosion. \\
\hline
{\em lee\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of lee-\/side erosion. \\
\hline
{\em uplift\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of uplift (orographic) effect. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+water\+\_\+depth} & Optional output\+: per-\/pixel water depth. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+inland\+\_\+mask} & Optional output\+: mask of inland pixels.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Heightmap array representing the generated island.
\end{DoxyReturn}

30.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{lee\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{uplift\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+water\+\_\+depth = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+inland\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates an island heightmap from a land mask using internally generated FBM noise for radial perturbation and slope modulation. 

Same as the other overload but creates a noise field procedurally from a seed, including frequency, octaves, orientation, and smoothing controls.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em land\+\_\+mask} & Binary mask defining the island shape. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Noise seed. \\
\hline
{\em noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of generated noise. \\
\hline
{\em noise\+\_\+kw} & Noise frequencies (x, y). \\
\hline
{\em noise\+\_\+octaves} & Number of FBM octaves. \\
\hline
{\em noise\+\_\+rugosity} & Persistence-\/like roughness control. \\
\hline
{\em noise\+\_\+angle} & Rotation of the noise field (radians). \\
\hline
{\em noise\+\_\+k\+\_\+smoothing} & Smoothing applied to the noise field. \\
\hline
{\em apex\+\_\+elevation} & Maximum elevation at island center. \\
\hline
{\em filter\+\_\+distance} & Enable smoothing of the distance transform. \\
\hline
{\em filter\+\_\+ir} & Radius of distance filter. \\
\hline
{\em slope\+\_\+min} & Minimum slope. \\
\hline
{\em slope\+\_\+max} & Maximum slope. \\
\hline
{\em slope\+\_\+start} & Start of slope ramp (0–1). \\
\hline
{\em slope\+\_\+end} & End of slope ramp (0–1). \\
\hline
{\em slope\+\_\+noise\+\_\+intensity} & Intensity of slope noise modulation. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smooth} & Smoothing factor for final profile. \\
\hline
{\em radial\+\_\+noise\+\_\+intensity} & Intensity of radial displacement noise. \\
\hline
{\em radial\+\_\+profile\+\_\+gain} & Exponent for radial falloff. \\
\hline
{\em water\+\_\+decay} & Transition sharpness to water level. \\
\hline
{\em water\+\_\+depth} & Water depth below the shoreline. \\
\hline
{\em lee\+\_\+angle} & Angle for lee-\/side erosion. \\
\hline
{\em lee\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude for lee-\/side erosion. \\
\hline
{\em uplift\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of uplift (orographic) effect. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+water\+\_\+depth} & Optional output\+: per-\/pixel water depth. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+inland\+\_\+mask} & Optional output\+: mask of inland pixels.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Heightmap array representing the generated island.
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::mountain\+\_\+cone (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape, 4.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{rugosity = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{angle = {\ttfamily 45.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smoothing = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{gamma = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{cone\+\_\+alpha = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{ridge\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.4\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{base\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.05\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{center = {\ttfamily \{0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a procedural "{}mountain cone"{} heightmap using fractal noise and Voronoi patterns. 

This function synthesizes a terrain-\/like array shaped as a cone with noise-\/based ridges and surface roughness. The generation combines a cone-\/shaped envelope ({\ttfamily cone\+\_\+sigmoid}), a fractal base noise ({\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a2c5d8132bf19f36c2934f17a3dcd1cf7}{gpu\+::noise\+\_\+fbm}}), and a Voronoi ridge structure ({\ttfamily voronoi\+\_\+fbm}), producing a mountain with controlled smoothness, angular distortion, and noise-\/based displacements.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & The output array dimensions (width, height). \\
\hline
{\em seed} & The random seed for noise generation. \\
\hline
{\em scale} & Global scaling factor for the mountain size. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of fractal noise octaves for both FBM and Voronoi. \\
\hline
{\em peak\+\_\+kw} & Controls the base frequency (inverse wavelength) of the peak noise. \\
\hline
{\em rugosity} & Controls the amplitude decay across octaves (higher = rougher surface). \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Direction (in degrees) for the displacement noise distortion. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smoothing} & Smoothing factor applied in Voronoi blending. \\
\hline
{\em gamma} & Gamma correction exponent applied at the end. \\
\hline
{\em cone\+\_\+alpha} & Controls the cone envelope steepness (higher = sharper peak). \\
\hline
{\em ridge\+\_\+amp} & Controls the amplitude of ridge enhancement in the Voronoi term. \\
\hline
{\em base\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude multiplier for the displacement noise. \\
\hline
{\em center} & The 2D position (in normalized coordinates) of the mountain cone center. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to an external X displacement noise field (can be nullptr). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to an external Y displacement noise field (can be nullptr). \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & The bounding box (min\+\_\+x, min\+\_\+y, max\+\_\+x, max\+\_\+y) defining the spatial extent of the map.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} representing the final terrain heightmap in normalized \mbox{[}0, 1\mbox{]} range.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mountain\_inselberg()}{mountain\_inselberg()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::mountain\+\_\+inselberg (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{scale = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{rugosity = {\ttfamily 45.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{gamma = {\ttfamily 1.1\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{round\+\_\+shape = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{bool}]{add\+\_\+deposition = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{bulk\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{base\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smoothing = {\ttfamily 0.1\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{center = {\ttfamily \{0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a synthetic mountain-\/like inselberg (isolated hill) heightmap. 

This function procedurally creates a 2D elevation field resembling an inselberg, using a combination of fractal noise (FBM), Gaussian pulses, and Voronoi-\/based structures. It allows control over scale, shape, orientation, rugosity, and optional geological-\/like effects such as bulk uplift and deposition smoothing.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Output array shape (resolution in x and y). \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed used for noise and Voronoi generation. \\
\hline
{\em scale} & Global scaling factor for the inselberg width and structure. \\
\hline
{\em rugosity} & Controls roughness of the fractal noise (higher = more irregular). \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Orientation angle (degrees) for directional displacements. \\
\hline
{\em gamma} & Gamma correction factor applied to the final heightmap. \\
\hline
{\em round\+\_\+shape} & If true, generates a symmetric round shape; if false, adds directional displacement. \\
\hline
{\em add\+\_\+deposition} & If true, applies a smoothing fill step simulating sediment deposition. \\
\hline
{\em bulk\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of bulk uplift applied to the base pulse (0 = none, \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}0 = raises and normalizes the feature). \\
\hline
{\em base\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of the base displacement noise. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smoothing} & Voronoi smoothing parameter (controls ridge sharpness). \\
\hline
{\em center} & Center of the inselberg in normalized coordinates. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to external displacement noise field (X-\/axis). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to external displacement noise field (Y-\/axis). \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box of the generation domain in normalized coordinates.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} containing the generated inselberg heightmap.
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::mountain\+\_\+range\+\_\+radial (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{half\+\_\+width = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{center = {\ttfamily \{0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{weight = {\ttfamily 0.7\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{persistence = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{lacunarity = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+angle = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a heightmap representing a radial mountain range. 

This function creates a heightmap that simulates a mountain range emanating radially from a specified center. The mountain range is influenced by various noise parameters and control attributes.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & The dimensions of the output heightmap as a 2D vector. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & The wave numbers (frequency components) as a 2D vector. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & The seed for random noise generation. \\
\hline
{\em half\+\_\+width} & The half-\/width of the radial mountain range, controlling its spread. Default is 0.\+2f. \\
\hline
{\em angle\+\_\+spread\+\_\+ratio} & The ratio controlling the angular spread of the mountain range. Default is 0.\+5f. \\
\hline
{\em center} & The center point of the radial mountain range as normalized coordinates within \mbox{[}0, 1\mbox{]}. Default is \{0.\+5f, 0.\+5f\}. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & The number of octaves for fractal noise generation. Default is 8. \\
\hline
{\em weight} & The initial weight for noise contribution. Default is 0.\+7f. \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & The amplitude scaling factor for subsequent noise octaves. Default is 0.\+5f. \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & The frequency scaling factor for subsequent noise octaves. Default is 2.\+0f. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & Optional pointer to an array of control parameters influencing the terrain generation. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to a precomputed noise array for the X-\/axis. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to a precomputed noise array for the Y-\/axis. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+angle} & Optional pointer to an array to output the angle. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & The bounding box of the output heightmap in normalized coordinates \mbox{[}xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax\mbox{]}. Default is \{0.\+0f, 1.\+0f, 0.\+0f, 1.\+0f\}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} The generated heightmap representing the radial mountain range.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::mountain\+\_\+stump (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{scale = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a mountain-\/like heightmap with a flattened (stump-\/shaped) peak. 

This function procedurally creates a terrain resembling a broad mountain with a smooth, truncated summit. The result combines layered fractal noise (FBM), Gaussian shaping, and Voronoi-\/based ridge formation to produce natural-\/looking geomorphological features. The shape can be modulated by directional displacement noise, smoothed using deposition simulation, and refined through gamma and smoothing parameters.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Dimensions of the output heightmap (width, height). \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed for noise generation. \\
\hline
{\em scale} & Global scale factor controlling the size of features. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of noise octaves used in FBM generation. \\
\hline
{\em peak\+\_\+kw} & Base spatial frequency of the main ridge/peak structure. \\
\hline
{\em rugosity} & Controls the roughness of base noise displacements. \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Orientation angle (in degrees) of the main ridge direction. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smoothing} & Smoothing coefficient applied to the Voronoi FBM ridges. \\
\hline
{\em gamma} & Gamma correction applied to the ridge intensity. \\
\hline
{\em add\+\_\+deposition} & If true, applies an additional smoothing pass to simulate sediment deposition. \\
\hline
{\em ridge\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude scaling factor for ridge prominence. \\
\hline
{\em base\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude scaling factor for base displacement noise. \\
\hline
{\em center} & Normalized coordinates of the mountain’s center (default domain\+: \mbox{[}0, 1\mbox{]}²). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to horizontal displacement noise (nullptr for none). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to vertical displacement noise (nullptr for none). \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box of the generated region (xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A 2D \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} containing the generated mountain stump heightmap.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a synthetic "{}\+Tibesti"{} mountain heightmap. 

This function procedurally creates a 2D elevation field inspired by the Tibesti mountains, a desert volcanic range. The terrain is built by combining Gabor wavelets, fractal simplex noise, and a Gaussian envelope, producing sharp volcanic peaks modulated by erosion-\/like patterns.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Output array shape (resolution in x and y). \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed used for noise and wavelet generation. \\
\hline
{\em scale} & Global scaling factor controlling the overall mountain size. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of octaves used in the fractal noise and Gabor FBM. \\
\hline
{\em peak\+\_\+kw} & Base frequency of the peak features (scaled internally by {\ttfamily scale}). \\
\hline
{\em rugosity} & Controls roughness of the fractal noise (higher = more irregular). \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Orientation angle (degrees) for Gabor waves. \\
\hline
{\em angle\+\_\+spread\+\_\+ratio} & Spread ratio of the Gabor wave orientation (controls anisotropy). \\
\hline
{\em gamma} & Gamma correction factor applied to auxiliary noise fields. \\
\hline
{\em add\+\_\+deposition} & If true, applies a smoothing fill step simulating sediment deposition. \\
\hline
{\em bulk\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of bulk uplift applied to the peaks (affects normalization with noise weighting). \\
\hline
{\em base\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of the base displacement noise. \\
\hline
{\em center} & Center of the mountain in normalized coordinates. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to external displacement noise field (X-\/axis). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to external displacement noise field (Y-\/axis). \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box of the generation domain in normalized coordinates.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} containing the generated Tibesti mountain heightmap.
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::multisteps (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{float}]{angle, 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{noise\+\_\+inflate = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{r = {\ttfamily 1.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{int}]{nsteps = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{elevation\+\_\+exponent = {\ttfamily {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const glm\+::vec2 \&}]{center = {\ttfamily \{0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{const glm\+::vec4 \&}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



GPU-\/accelerated multi-\/step height generation with procedural noise. 

Builds the same multi-\/step profile as the CPU version but injects a Voronoi-\/\+FBM noise field to modulate the step positions. Noise can be inflated or deflated and is projected onto the step axis before being passed to the CPU \doxylink{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_aaa93c5f0c20e23dfb4d0f67b99489178}{multisteps()} implementation.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Output array resolution. \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Rotation angle in degrees. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Noise seed. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Base wave numbers for noise. \\
\hline
{\em noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of injected noise. \\
\hline
{\em noise\+\_\+rugosity} & Roughness of the FBM noise. \\
\hline
{\em noise\+\_\+inflate} & Whether to invert noise direction. \\
\hline
{\em r} & Geometric ratio between steps. \\
\hline
{\em nsteps} & Number of steps. \\
\hline
{\em elevation\+\_\+exponent} & Exponent shaping step heights. \\
\hline
{\em shape\+\_\+gain} & Gain used to reshape intra-\/step transitions. \\
\hline
{\em scale} & Scale of the step axis. \\
\hline
{\em outer\+\_\+slope} & Slope outside the \mbox{[}0,1\mbox{]} axis interval. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & Optional control parameter array. \\
\hline
{\em center} & Center of the step axis. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box of the domain. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Generated \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{phasor()}{phasor()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::phasor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a67d6620c147710ebb09b64f0f738241a}{Phasor\+Profile}}}]{phasor\+\_\+profile,  }\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{float}]{kp\+\_\+global,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{angle\+\_\+shift = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{int}]{n\+\_\+kernel\+\_\+samples = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{const glm\+::vec2}]{jitter = {\ttfamily \{1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{int}]{angle\+\_\+filter\+\_\+ir = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{delta = {\ttfamily 0.01\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{phase\+\_\+smoothing = {\ttfamily 10.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+angle = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a procedural phasor-\/based pattern. 

Produces a directional, phase-\/driven field using a selected profile, optional angle control, and spatial distortion noise.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em phasor\+\_\+profile} & Phasor shaping profile. \\
\hline
{\em shape} & Output array dimensions. \\
\hline
{\em kp\+\_\+global} & Global frequency factor. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed. \\
\hline
{\em angle\+\_\+shift} & Global phase angle offset (degrees). \\
\hline
{\em n\+\_\+kernel\+\_\+samples} & Number of kernel samples. \\
\hline
{\em jitter} & Sampling jitter (x,y). \\
\hline
{\em angle\+\_\+filter\+\_\+ir} & Angular filtering radius. \\
\hline
{\em delta} & Finite difference step. \\
\hline
{\em phase\+\_\+smoothing} & Phase smoothing factor. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+angle} & Optional external angle field. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional X distortion field. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional Y distortion field. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Domain bounding box. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} Generated phasor field.
\end{DoxyReturn}

(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a67d6620c147710ebb09b64f0f738241a}{Phasor\+Profile}}}]{phasor\+\_\+profile,  }\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a multi-\/octave (f\+Bm) phasor-\/based pattern. 

Accumulates several scaled {\ttfamily phasor} layers using persistence and lacunarity for richer multi-\/scale structure.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em phasor\+\_\+profile} & Phasor shaping profile. \\
\hline
{\em shape} & Output array dimensions. \\
\hline
{\em kp\+\_\+global} & Base frequency factor. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed. \\
\hline
{\em angle\+\_\+shift} & Global phase angle offset (degrees). \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of f\+Bm layers. \\
\hline
{\em weight} & Initial octave weight. \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & Amplitude multiplier per octave. \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & Frequency multiplier per octave. \\
\hline
{\em n\+\_\+kernel\+\_\+samples} & Number of kernel samples. \\
\hline
{\em jitter} & Sampling jitter (x,y). \\
\hline
{\em angle\+\_\+filter\+\_\+ir} & Angular filtering radius. \\
\hline
{\em delta} & Finite difference step. \\
\hline
{\em phase\+\_\+smoothing} & Phase smoothing factor. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+angle} & Optional external angle field. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional X distortion field. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional Y distortion field. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Domain bounding box. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} Generated multi-\/scale phasor field.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{plates@{plates}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{plates()}{plates()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::plates (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{talus,  }\item[{int}]{direction = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{float}]{mix\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 0.9\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{base\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.05\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{kw\+\_\+multiplier = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{rugosity = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generate a tectonic plate–like heightfield using Voronoi FBM and directional talus projection. 

Combines Voronoi edge-\/distance FBM with a base noise displacement, then applies a talus projection along a given direction and blends the result with the original field.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Grid resolution. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Base wavelength/frequency. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed. \\
\hline
{\em talus} & Talus strength for directional projection. \\
\hline
{\em direction} & Projection direction. \\
\hline
{\em mix\+\_\+ratio} & Blend factor between raw Voronoi and projected plates. \\
\hline
{\em base\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of the displacement noise. \\
\hline
{\em kw\+\_\+multiplier} & Frequency multiplier for base noise. \\
\hline
{\em rugosity} & Noise roughness. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box for noise evaluation. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Generated plate heightfield.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{polygon\_field()}{polygon\_field()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::polygon\+\_\+field (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{rmin = {\ttfamily  }\item[{float}]{density = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{jitter = {\ttfamily \{0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{float}]{shift = {\ttfamily 0.1\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+distance = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+density\+\_\+multiplier = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+size\+\_\+multiplier = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a scalar field representing the signed distance to randomly generated polygons. 

This function procedurally generates a field where each pixel stores the signed distance to the nearest polygon, using a smooth signed distance function (SDF) with optional clamping. The polygons are generated randomly within the specified bounding box, with configurable vertex counts, sizes, jitter, and density. Optionally, displacement noise fields can be applied to polygon positions.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Resolution of the output field (width, height). \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Scaling factor for field coordinates (world units per pixel). \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed for polygon generation. \\
\hline
{\em rmin} & Minimum polygon radius (relative to bbox size). \\
\hline
{\em rmax} & Maximum polygon radius (relative to bbox size). \\
\hline
{\em clamping\+\_\+dist} & Distance threshold for clamping the SDF value (used to soften edges). \\
\hline
{\em clamping\+\_\+k} & Smoothness parameter for clamping. \\
\hline
{\em n\+\_\+vertices\+\_\+min} & Minimum number of vertices per polygon. \\
\hline
{\em n\+\_\+vertices\+\_\+max} & Maximum number of vertices per polygon. \\
\hline
{\em density} & Fraction of pixels covered by polygons (approximate). \\
\hline
{\em jitter} & Random displacement factor applied to polygon vertices. \\
\hline
{\em shift} & Random position shift applied to polygon center. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional displacement noise field in the X direction (nullptr to disable). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional displacement noise field in the Y direction (nullptr to disable). \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box in normalized coordinates \{xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax\}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} 2D array containing the signed distance field.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Polygons are randomly generated per call and are not guaranteed to be convex. 

The sign of the SDF is negative inside polygons and positive outside.
\end{DoxyNote}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}

= {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a scalar field representing the signed distance to randomly generated polygons combined with fractal Brownian motion (f\+Bm) noise modulation. 

Similar to \doxylink{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_ac7c2489dd7079a4904b481815bb7dd0d}{polygon\+\_\+field()}, but the generated SDF is modulated by an f\+Bm noise function to create more natural, irregular shapes. The f\+Bm parameters allow control over the noise persistence, lacunarity, and number of octaves.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Resolution of the output field (width, height). \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Scaling factor for field coordinates (world units per pixel). \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed for polygon generation and f\+Bm noise. \\
\hline
{\em rmin} & Minimum polygon radius (relative to bbox size). \\
\hline
{\em rmax} & Maximum polygon radius (relative to bbox size). \\
\hline
{\em clamping\+\_\+dist} & Distance threshold for clamping the SDF value (used to soften edges). \\
\hline
{\em clamping\+\_\+k} & Smoothness parameter for clamping. \\
\hline
{\em n\+\_\+vertices\+\_\+min} & Minimum number of vertices per polygon. \\
\hline
{\em n\+\_\+vertices\+\_\+max} & Maximum number of vertices per polygon. \\
\hline
{\em density} & Fraction of pixels covered by polygons (approximate). \\
\hline
{\em jitter} & Random displacement factor applied to polygon vertices. \\
\hline
{\em shift} & Random position shift applied to polygon center. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of f\+Bm octaves. \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & Amplitude decay per octave in f\+Bm. \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & Frequency multiplier per octave in f\+Bm. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional displacement noise field in the X direction (nullptr to disable). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional displacement noise field in the Y direction (nullptr to disable). \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box in normalized coordinates \{xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax\}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} 2D array containing the signed distance field modulated by f\+Bm.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The sign of the SDF is negative inside polygons and positive outside.
\end{DoxyNote}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::shattered\+\_\+peak (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{scale = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a synthetic "{}shattered peak"{} terrain heightmap. 

This function procedurally creates a 2D elevation field resembling a sharp, fractured mountain peak. It combines a Gaussian pulse envelope, fractal noise displacements, and Voronoi-\/based primitives with edge-\/distance shaping. The result is a rugged peak structure with broken ridges and steep slopes.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Output array shape (resolution in x and y). \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed used for noise and Voronoi generation. \\
\hline
{\em scale} & Global scaling factor controlling the overall peak size. \\
\hline
{\em peak\+\_\+kw} & Base frequency of the peak features (scaled internally by {\ttfamily scale}). \\
\hline
{\em rugosity} & Controls roughness of the fractal noise (higher = more irregular). \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Orientation angle (degrees) for directional displacements. \\
\hline
{\em gamma} & Gamma correction factor applied to the final heightmap. \\
\hline
{\em add\+\_\+deposition} & If true, applies a smoothing fill step simulating sediment deposition. \\
\hline
{\em bulk\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of bulk uplift applied to the peak (internally overridden to 0.\+5f for normalization). \\
\hline
{\em base\+\_\+noise\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of the base displacement noise. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smoothing} & Voronoi smoothing parameter (controls ridge sharpness). \\
\hline
{\em center} & Center of the peak in normalized coordinates. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to external displacement noise field (X-\/axis). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to external displacement noise field (Y-\/axis). \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box of the generation domain in normalized coordinates.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} containing the generated shattered peak heightmap.
\end{DoxyReturn}
{\bfseries{Example}}

{\bfseries{Result}}  \Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a845e5938c39cdab886b3e354cb53d078}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a845e5938c39cdab886b3e354cb53d078}

\index{vorolines@{vorolines}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vorolines()}{vorolines()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::vorolines (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{float}]{density,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smoothing = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{exp\+\_\+sigma = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{alpha = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{alpha\+\_\+span = {\ttfamily M\+\_\+PI},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2f}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type}}}]{return\+\_\+type = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2fa3e5996ed4314058911435c50bc95e1c2}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type\+::\+F1\+\_\+\+SQUARED}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox\+\_\+points = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a Voronoi-\/based pattern where cells are defined by proximity to random lines. 

This function generates an Open\+CL-\/accelerated Voronoi-\/like pattern based on the distance from each pixel to a set of randomly oriented lines. Each line is defined by a random point and a direction sampled from a uniform distribution around a given angle.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & The resolution of the resulting 2D array (width, height). \\
\hline
{\em density} & Number of base points per unit area used to define lines. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Seed for the random number generator used to generate base points and directions. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smoothing} & Kernel smoothing factor; controls how sharp or soft the distance fields are. \\
\hline
{\em exp\+\_\+sigma} & Exponential smoothing parameter applied to the computed distance field. \\
\hline
{\em alpha} & Base angle (in radians) used to orient the generated lines. \\
\hline
{\em alpha\+\_\+span} & Maximum angular deviation from {\ttfamily alpha}; controls line orientation variability. \\
\hline
{\em return\+\_\+type} & Type of Voronoi output to return (e.\+g., F1, F2, edge distance, smoothed field, etc.). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to an input noise field applied to the X coordinates (can be nullptr). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to an input noise field applied to the Y coordinates (can be nullptr). \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box in normalized coordinates (min\+\_\+x, max\+\_\+x, min\+\_\+y, max\+\_\+y) of the final array. \\
\hline
{\em bbox\+\_\+points} & Bounding box within which random base points are sampled.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A 2D array (of type \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}) containing the computed distance field based on line proximity.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Each line is defined from a point (x, y) to a direction offset using angle {\ttfamily theta = alpha + rand \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} alpha\+\_\+span}. 

The Open\+CL kernel "{}vorolines"{} must be defined and compiled beforehand.
\end{DoxyNote}
{\bfseries{Example}}

{\bfseries{Result}}   \Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_acc7dccf4ab556f489ffbaef1592fe375}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_acc7dccf4ab556f489ffbaef1592fe375} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!vorolines\_fbm@{vorolines\_fbm}}
\index{vorolines\_fbm@{vorolines\_fbm}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vorolines\_fbm()}{vorolines\_fbm()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::vorolines\+\_\+fbm (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{float}]{density,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smoothing = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{exp\+\_\+sigma = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{alpha = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{alpha\+\_\+span = {\ttfamily M\+\_\+PI},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2f}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type}}}]{return\+\_\+type = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2fa3e5996ed4314058911435c50bc95e1c2}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type\+::\+F1\+\_\+\+SQUARED}}},  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{weight = {\ttfamily 0.7\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{persistence = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{lacunarity = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox\+\_\+points = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a Voronoi-\/based pattern using distances to lines defined by random points and angles, with additional fractal Brownian motion (f\+Bm) noise modulation. 

This function extends the standard {\ttfamily vorolines} generation by introducing f\+Bm-\/based warping of the coordinate space, resulting in more organic and fractal-\/like structures. It creates a Voronoi distance field based on proximity to oriented line segments and distorts the result using multi-\/octave procedural noise.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Output resolution of the 2D array (width, height). \\
\hline
{\em density} & Number of base points per unit area used to define lines. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Seed value for the random number generator. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smoothing} & Kernel smoothing coefficient to soften distance values (e.\+g., for blending). \\
\hline
{\em exp\+\_\+sigma} & Sigma value for optional exponential smoothing on the final field. \\
\hline
{\em alpha} & Base orientation angle (in radians) of lines generated from random points. \\
\hline
{\em alpha\+\_\+span} & Maximum angle deviation from {\ttfamily alpha}, determining directional randomness of lines. \\
\hline
{\em return\+\_\+type} & Type of output to return (e.\+g., F1, F2, distance to edge, smoothed version). \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of noise octaves used in the f\+Bm modulation. \\
\hline
{\em weight} & Weight of each octave\textquotesingle{}s contribution to the total noise. \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & Amplitude decay factor for each successive octave (commonly 0.\+5–0.8). \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & Frequency multiplier for each successive octave (commonly 2.\+0). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to an external noise field applied to X coordinates (can be nullptr). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to an external noise field applied to Y coordinates (can be nullptr). \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box for the final image domain (min\+\_\+x, max\+\_\+x, min\+\_\+y, max\+\_\+y). \\
\hline
{\em bbox\+\_\+points} & Bounding box from which the initial set of points are sampled.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A 2D {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} representing the Voronoi-\/f\+Bm field, distorted by noise and influenced by distance to random lines.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This version uses internally computed f\+Bm noise unless external fields ({\ttfamily p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x}, {\ttfamily p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y}) are provided. 

This function requires an Open\+CL kernel named "{}vorolines\+\_\+fbm"{} to be compiled and accessible.
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{voronoi()}{voronoi()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::voronoi (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{jitter = {\ttfamily \{0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smoothing = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{exp\+\_\+sigma = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2f}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type}}}]{return\+\_\+type = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2fa3e5996ed4314058911435c50bc95e1c2}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type\+::\+F1\+\_\+\+SQUARED}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a Voronoi diagram in a 2D array with configurable properties. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & The dimensions of the output array as a 2D vector of integers. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & The frequency scale factors for the Voronoi cells, given as a 2D vector of floats. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & A seed value for random number generation, ensuring reproducibility. \\
\hline
{\em jitter} & (Optional) The amount of random variation in the positions of Voronoi cell sites, given as a 2D vector of floats. Defaults to \{0.\+5f, 0.\+5f\}. \\
\hline
{\em return\+\_\+type} & (Optional) The type of value to compute for the Voronoi diagram. Defaults to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2fa3e5996ed4314058911435c50bc95e1c2}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type\+::\+F1\+\_\+\+SQUARED}}. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & (Optional) A pointer to an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} used to control the Voronoi computation. Used here as a multiplier for the jitter. If nullptr, no control is applied. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & (Optional) A pointer to an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} providing additional noise in the x-\/direction for cell positions. If nullptr, no x-\/noise is applied. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & (Optional) A pointer to an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} providing additional noise in the y-\/direction for cell positions. If nullptr, no y-\/noise is applied. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & (Optional) The bounding box for the Voronoi computation, given as a 4D vector of floats representing \{min\+\_\+x, max\+\_\+x, min\+\_\+y, max\+\_\+y\}. Defaults to \{0.\+f, 1.\+f, 0.\+f, 1.\+f\}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A 2D array representing the generated Voronoi diagram.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{voronoi\_fbm@{voronoi\_fbm}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{voronoi\_fbm()}{voronoi\_fbm()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::voronoi\+\_\+fbm (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{jitter = {\ttfamily \{0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smoothing = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{exp\+\_\+sigma = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2f}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type}}}]{return\+\_\+type = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2fa3e5996ed4314058911435c50bc95e1c2}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type\+::\+F1\+\_\+\+SQUARED}}},  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{weight = {\ttfamily 0.7\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{persistence = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{lacunarity = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a Voronoi diagram in a 2D array with configurable properties. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & The dimensions of the output array as a 2D vector of integers. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & The frequency scale factors for the base Voronoi cells, given as a 2D vector of floats. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & A seed value for random number generation, ensuring reproducibility. \\
\hline
{\em jitter} & (Optional) The amount of random variation in the positions of Voronoi cell sites, given as a 2D vector of floats. Defaults to \{0.\+5f, 0.\+5f\}. \\
\hline
{\em return\+\_\+type} & (Optional) The type of value to compute for the Voronoi diagram. Defaults to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2fa3e5996ed4314058911435c50bc95e1c2}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type\+::\+F1\+\_\+\+SQUARED}}. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & (Optional) The number of layers (octaves) in the fractal Brownian motion. Defaults to 8. \\
\hline
{\em weight} & (Optional) The initial weight of the base layer in the FBM computation. Defaults to 0.\+7f. \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & (Optional) The persistence factor that controls the amplitude reduction between octaves. Defaults to 0.\+5f. \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & (Optional) The lacunarity factor that controls the frequency increase between octaves. Defaults to 2.\+f. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & (Optional) A pointer to an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} used to control the Voronoi computation. If nullptr, no control is applied. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & (Optional) A pointer to an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} providing additional noise in the x-\/direction for cell positions. If nullptr, no x-\/noise is applied. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & (Optional) A pointer to an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} providing additional noise in the y-\/direction for cell positions. If nullptr, no y-\/noise is applied. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & (Optional) The bounding box for the Voronoi computation, given as a 4D vector of floats representing \{min\+\_\+x, max\+\_\+x, min\+\_\+y, max\+\_\+y\}. Defaults to \{0.\+f, 1.\+f, 0.\+f, 1.\+f\}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A 2D array representing the generated Voronoi diagram.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{voronoi\_edge\_distance()}{voronoi\_edge\_distance()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::voronoi\+\_\+edge\+\_\+distance (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{jitter = {\ttfamily \{0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes the Voronoi edge distance. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & The shape of the grid as a 2D vector (width, height). \\
\hline
{\em kw} & The weights for the Voronoi kernel as a 2D vector. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & The random seed used for generating Voronoi points. \\
\hline
{\em jitter} & Optional parameter for controlling jitter in Voronoi point placement (default is \{0.\+5f, 0.\+5f\}). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & Optional pointer to an \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} specifying control parameters for Voronoi grid jitter (default is nullptr). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x,p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Reference to the input noise arrays. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & The bounding box for the Voronoi diagram as \{x\+\_\+min, x\+\_\+max, y\+\_\+min, y\+\_\+max\} (default is \{0.\+f, 1.\+f, 0.\+f, 1.\+f\}).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Taken from \href{https://www.shadertoy.com/view/llG3zy}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+shadertoy.\+com/view/ll\+G3zy}}

Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.

The resulting \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} has the same dimensions as the input shape. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_aafc7d621ebf149a27f287222127294ab}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_aafc7d621ebf149a27f287222127294ab} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!voronoise@{voronoise}}
\index{voronoise@{voronoise}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{voronoise()}{voronoise()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::voronoise (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{float}]{u\+\_\+param,  }\item[{float}]{v\+\_\+param,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a 2D Voronoi noise array. 

This function computes a Voronoi noise pattern based on the input parameters and returns it as a 2D array. The noise is calculated in the Open\+CL kernel {\ttfamily noise\+\_\+voronoise}, which uses a combination of hashing and smoothstep functions to generate a weighted Voronoi noise field.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Taken from \href{https://www.shadertoy.com/view/Xd23Dh}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+shadertoy.\+com/view/\+Xd23\+Dh}}

Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & The dimensions of the 2D output array as a vector (width and height). \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Wave numbers for scaling the noise pattern, represented as a 2D vector. \\
\hline
{\em u\+\_\+param} & A control parameter for the noise, adjusting the contribution of random offsets. \\
\hline
{\em v\+\_\+param} & A control parameter for the noise, affecting the smoothness of the pattern. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & Optional pointer to an \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} specifying control parameters for Voronoi grid jitter (default is nullptr). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x,p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Reference to the input noise arrays. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & A seed value for random number generation, ensuring reproducibility.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} object containing the generated 2D Voronoi noise values.
\end{DoxyReturn}
