{\bfseries{Result}}  \Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_af15ee9a79a551cf83cdabdadc2065cf5}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_af15ee9a79a551cf83cdabdadc2065cf5} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!vororand@{vororand}}
\index{vororand@{vororand}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vororand()}{vororand()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::vororand (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{float}]{density,  }\item[{float}]{variability,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smoothing = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{exp\+\_\+sigma = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2f}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type}}}]{return\+\_\+type = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2fa3e5996ed4314058911435c50bc95e1c2}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type\+::\+F1\+\_\+\+SQUARED}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox\+\_\+points = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a 2D Voronoi-\/based scalar field using Open\+CL. 

This function computes a Voronoi diagram or derived metric (such as F1, F2, or edge distances) on a grid of given shape. A set of random points is generated within an extended bounding box, based on the desired density and variability, to reduce edge artifacts. Optionally, per-\/pixel displacement can be applied through noise fields.

The result is stored in an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} object representing a 2D scalar field.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Dimensions of the output array (width x height). \\
\hline
{\em density} & Number of random points per unit area for Voronoi diagram. \\
\hline
{\em variability} & Amount of randomness added to the point generation bounding box. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Seed for random number generation used in point sampling. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smoothing} & Smoothing factor used in soft minimum/maximum Voronoi distance computations. \\
\hline
{\em exp\+\_\+sigma} & Standard deviation used in exponential falloff for edge distance computation. \\
\hline
{\em return\+\_\+type} & Type of Voronoi computation to perform (e.\+g., F1, F2, F2-\/\+F1, edge distance). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to a noise field applied to X coordinates of grid points. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to a noise field applied to Y coordinates of grid points. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box of the domain in which the field is computed\+: \{xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax\}. \\
\hline
{\em bbox\+\_\+points} & Bounding box for point generation, usually larger than {\ttfamily bbox} to avoid edge effects.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} object containing the computed scalar field.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The kernel {\ttfamily "{}vororand"{}} must be compiled and available in the Open\+CL context.
\item If {\ttfamily p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} or {\ttfamily p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} are provided, they must match the shape of the output array.
\item The generated point cloud will be larger than {\ttfamily bbox} to reduce border artifacts.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

{\bfseries{Result}}  \Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a33d9640c06dfec4032dbf8b2116ff803}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a33d9640c06dfec4032dbf8b2116ff803}

\index{vororand@{vororand}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vororand()}{vororand()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::vororand (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{const std\+::vector$<$ float $>$ \&}]{xp,  }\item[{const std\+::vector$<$ float $>$ \&}]{yp,  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smoothing = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{exp\+\_\+sigma = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2f}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type}}}]{return\+\_\+type = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2fa3e5996ed4314058911435c50bc95e1c2}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type\+::\+F1\+\_\+\+SQUARED}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a3e358c95d75cd4df78381a7d6700c2fd}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a3e358c95d75cd4df78381a7d6700c2fd} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!wavelet\_noise@{wavelet\_noise}}
\index{wavelet\_noise@{wavelet\_noise}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wavelet\_noise()}{wavelet\_noise()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::wavelet\+\_\+noise (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{glm\+::ivec2}]{shape,  }\item[{glm\+::vec2}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{kw\+\_\+multiplier = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{vorticity = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{density = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{weight = {\ttfamily 0.7\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{persistence = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{lacunarity = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{glm\+::vec4}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates 2D wavelet noise using an Open\+CL kernel. 

This function creates a 2D noise field of the given {\ttfamily shape} using multi-\/octave wavelet turbulence. The noise is computed on the GPU via the "{}wavelet\+\_\+noise"{} Open\+CL kernel. Various parameters control the frequency evolution, amplitude decay, vorticity injection, and optional modulation using additional input arrays.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Resolution of the output noise array (width, height). \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Base wave number (frequency) in each axis. Controls the initial spatial frequency of the wavelet field. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Integer seed used by the random hashing functions inside the kernel. \\
\hline
{\em kw\+\_\+multiplier} & Multiplier applied to the wave number per octave (similar to gain). Higher values increase frequency growth across octaves. \\
\hline
{\em vorticity} & Amount of rotational distortion injected into the noise. When \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0, the kernel applies additional angular perturbations to produce turbulent flow-\/like patterns. \\
\hline
{\em density} & Global scaling factor controlling the overall contrast or amplitude of the generated noise. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of wavelet noise layers combined. Higher octaves yield more detail but increase computational cost. \\
\hline
{\em weight} & Weight applied to the base octave, used as a global intensity multiplier before persistence attenuation is applied. \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & Amplitude decay factor per octave. Values in (0,1) produce the classic fractal noise falloff; higher values retain more high-\/frequency detail. \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & Frequency multiplier per octave. Controls how rapidly frequency increases at each octave, with typical values in the range \mbox{[}1.\+5, 3.\+0\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & Optional pointer to a control-\/parameter array. When provided, values inside this array modulate the generated noise spatially. Pass nullptr to disable this feature. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to an auxiliary noise array used to perturb sampling positions horizontally. Pass nullptr to disable. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to an auxiliary noise array used to perturb sampling positions vertically. Pass nullptr to disable. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding-\/box mapping (xmin, ymin, xmax, ymax). Converts pixel-\/space indices into world-\/space coordinates for spatially consistent noise.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} A 2D floating-\/point array containing the generated wavelet noise.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{select\_soil\_flow()}{select\_soil\_flow()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::select\+\_\+soil\+\_\+flow (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{int}]{ir\+\_\+gradient = {\ttfamily 1},  }\item[{float}]{gradient\+\_\+weight = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{gradient\+\_\+scaling\+\_\+factor = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{flow\+\_\+weight = {\ttfamily 0.05\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{talus\+\_\+ref = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{clipping\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 50.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{flow\+\_\+gamma = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smooth = {\ttfamily 0.01\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes a soil–flow selection map based on terrain gradient, river mask, and smoothing parameters. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Input heightmap. \\
\hline
{\em ir\+\_\+gradient} & Radius used for the morphological gradient. \\
\hline
{\em gradient\+\_\+weight} & Weight applied to the gradient magnitude. \\
\hline
{\em gradient\+\_\+scaling\+\_\+factor} & Scaling factor applied to the gradient; defaults to z.\+shape.\+x if \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= 0. \\
\hline
{\em talus\+\_\+ref} & Reference talus value for river extraction; defaults to 1.\+f / z.\+shape.\+x if \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= 0. \\
\hline
{\em clipping\+\_\+ratio} & Clipping ratio used in the river selection step. \\
\hline
{\em flow\+\_\+gamma} & Gamma correction exponent applied to the river mask; 1.\+0 disables correction. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smooth} & Smoothing parameter for the maximum blending.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A 2D \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} representing the final soil-\/flow selection mask.
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\bfseries{Result}}  \Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a735421f1b5f42ade55224b932603c58e}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a735421f1b5f42ade55224b932603c58e} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!select\_soil\_rocks@{select\_soil\_rocks}}
\index{select\_soil\_rocks@{select\_soil\_rocks}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{select\_soil\_rocks()}{select\_soil\_rocks()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::select\+\_\+soil\+\_\+rocks (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{int}]{ir\+\_\+max = {\ttfamily 64},  }\item[{int}]{ir\+\_\+min = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{int}]{steps = {\ttfamily 4},  }\item[{float}]{smaller\+\_\+scales\+\_\+weight = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_ad4876bd26d1f3b33a1492645bfe50fbe}{Clamp\+Mode}}}]{curvature\+\_\+clamp\+\_\+mode = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_ad4876bd26d1f3b33a1492645bfe50fbea7ee5673a01d4215ae4ba9ba95268ed59}{Clamp\+Mode\+::\+POSITIVE\+\_\+\+ONLY}}},  }\item[{float}]{curvature\+\_\+clamping = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes a multi-\/scale soil/rock selector using curvature analysis. 

Applies progressively increasing smoothing radii in logarithmic steps (handling ir\+\_\+min = 0), computes the mean curvature at each scale, clamps it, and accumulates the maximum response across all scales.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Input heightmap or scalar field. \\
\hline
{\em ir\+\_\+max} & Maximum smoothing radius (log-\/scale upper bound). \\
\hline
{\em ir\+\_\+min} & Minimum smoothing radius (0 allowed; replaced by 1 for log scale). \\
\hline
{\em steps} & Number of logarithmic scales to evaluate. \\
\hline
{\em smaller\+\_\+scales\+\_\+weight} & Weight factor applied when descending scales. \\
\hline
{\em curvature\+\_\+clamp\+\_\+mode} & Mode used to clamp curvature values. \\
\hline
{\em curvature\+\_\+clamping} & Curvature clamp threshold.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} representing soil/rock selection values across scales.
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\bfseries{Result}}  \Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_ae394dd88c39510d2ada01cf120922719}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_ae394dd88c39510d2ada01cf120922719} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!select\_soil\_weathered@{select\_soil\_weathered}}
\index{select\_soil\_weathered@{select\_soil\_weathered}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{select\_soil\_weathered()}{select\_soil\_weathered()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::select\+\_\+soil\+\_\+weathered (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{int}]{ir\+\_\+curvature = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{int}]{ir\+\_\+gradient = {\ttfamily 4},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_ad4876bd26d1f3b33a1492645bfe50fbe}{Clamp\+Mode}}}]{curvature\+\_\+clamp\+\_\+mode = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_ad4876bd26d1f3b33a1492645bfe50fbea7ee5673a01d4215ae4ba9ba95268ed59}{Clamp\+Mode\+::\+POSITIVE\+\_\+\+ONLY}}},  }\item[{float}]{curvature\+\_\+clamping = {\ttfamily 10.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{curvature\+\_\+weight = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{gradient\+\_\+weight = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{gradient\+\_\+scaling\+\_\+factor = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes a soil weathering selection map based on curvature and gradient analysis. 

This function generates a combined array representing the degree of soil weathering using two main components\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Curvature contribution}}\+: derived from smoothed height variations.
\item {\bfseries{Gradient contribution}}\+: derived from local slope magnitudes.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Input heightmap or scalar field. \\
\hline
{\em ir\+\_\+curvature} & Radius (in pixels or samples) for curvature smoothing. If zero, curvature smoothing is skipped. \\
\hline
{\em ir\+\_\+gradient} & Radius (in pixels or samples) for gradient computation. \\
\hline
{\em curvature\+\_\+clamp\+\_\+mode} & Clamping mode applied to curvature values (see \doxylink{namespacehmap_ad4876bd26d1f3b33a1492645bfe50fbe}{Clamp\+Mode}). \\
\hline
{\em curvature\+\_\+clamping} & Maximum absolute value used for curvature clamping. \\
\hline
{\em curvature\+\_\+weight} & Weight applied to the curvature component in the final mix. \\
\hline
{\em gradient\+\_\+weight} & Weight applied to the gradient component in the final mix. \\
\hline
{\em gradient\+\_\+scaling\+\_\+factor} & Empirical scaling factor for both curvature and gradient terms. If non-\/positive, defaults to {\ttfamily z.\+shape.\+x}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::select\+\_\+soil\+\_\+weathered (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{gradient\+\_\+norm,  }\item[{int}]{ir\+\_\+curvature,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_ad4876bd26d1f3b33a1492645bfe50fbe}{Clamp\+Mode}}}]{curvature\+\_\+clamp\+\_\+mode,  }\item[{float}]{curvature\+\_\+clamping,  }\item[{float}]{curvature\+\_\+weight,  }\item[{float}]{gradient\+\_\+weight,  }\item[{float}]{gradient\+\_\+scaling\+\_\+factor }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a13f97a9cf5f7f219e5ed9a32fefbfa1a}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a13f97a9cf5f7f219e5ed9a32fefbfa1a}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a12757ceaaf11f04640c3a18520886cc8}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a12757ceaaf11f04640c3a18520886cc8} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!advection\_particle@{advection\_particle}}
\index{advection\_particle@{advection\_particle}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{advection\_particle()}{advection\_particle()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::advection\+\_\+particle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{advected\+\_\+field,  }\item[{int}]{iterations,  }\item[{int}]{nparticles,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{bool}]{reverse = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{bool}]{post\+\_\+filter = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{post\+\_\+filter\+\_\+sigma = {\ttfamily 0.125\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{advection\+\_\+length = {\ttfamily 0.1\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{value\+\_\+persistence = {\ttfamily 0.99\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{inertia = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+advection\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs particle-\/based advection on a scalar field. 

This function advects particles through a velocity field (or gradient field) derived from the input array {\ttfamily z}. Each particle carries a value from the {\ttfamily advected\+\_\+field} and evolves over a number of iterations according to advection parameters such as inertia and persistence. Optionally, advection and masking fields can be applied to control which areas are affected.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & Input scalar field defining the base flow or gradient field used for particle advection. \\
\hline
{\em advected\+\_\+field} & The scalar field whose values are transported along particle trajectories. \\
\hline
{\em iterations} & Number of advection iterations to perform per particle. \\
\hline
{\em nparticles} & Number of particles to simulate during advection. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed used for initializing particle positions and stochastic behavior. \\
\hline
{\em reverse} & If true, reverses the advection direction (useful for backtracing or inverse advection). \\
\hline
{\em post\+\_\+filter} & If true, applies a smoothing or filtering operation after advection to reduce artifacts. \\
\hline
{\em advection\+\_\+length} & Maximum advection step length per iteration (controls particle displacement scale). \\
\hline
{\em value\+\_\+persistence} & Controls how much of a particle’s advected value is preserved between iterations (1.\+0 means full preservation, lower values introduce decay). \\
\hline
{\em inertia} & Controls how much a particle’s previous velocity affects its next step (simulates momentum). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+advection\+\_\+mask} & Optional mask array controlling where advection occurs (nullptr to disable). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+mask} & Optional general mask restricting where output values are written (nullptr to disable).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} representing the advected version of {\ttfamily advected\+\_\+field} after applying particle advection.
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::advection\+\_\+particle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{dx,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{dy,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{advected\+\_\+field,  }\item[{int}]{nparticles,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{bool}]{reverse = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{bool}]{post\+\_\+filter = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{post\+\_\+filter\+\_\+sigma = {\ttfamily 0.125\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{advection\+\_\+length = {\ttfamily 0.1\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{value\+\_\+persistence = {\ttfamily 0.99\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{inertia = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+advection\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a6e5f495c359df88d1185220ab1cc8c23}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a6e5f495c359df88d1185220ab1cc8c23} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!advection\_warp@{advection\_warp}}
\index{advection\_warp@{advection\_warp}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{advection\_warp()}{advection\_warp()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::advection\+\_\+warp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{advected\+\_\+field,  }\item[{float}]{advection\+\_\+length = {\ttfamily 0.1\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{value\+\_\+persistence = {\ttfamily 0.9\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs 2D field advection based on the gradient of a heightmap using a warp-\/based technic (simplified approach). 

This function computes the X and Y gradients of the given heightmap {\ttfamily z} and uses them as flow directions to advect the input {\ttfamily advected\+\_\+field}. The result is a new field where values have been displaced according to the gradient direction and the specified advection parameters.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em z} & The heightmap (or scalar field) used to compute advection directions. \\
\hline
{\em advected\+\_\+field} & The field to be advected along the gradient of {\ttfamily z}. \\
\hline
{\em advection\+\_\+length} & The step length used for advection; larger values produce stronger displacement. \\
\hline
{\em value\+\_\+persistence} & The persistence factor applied to the advected values, typically in the range \mbox{[}0, 1\mbox{]}; controls how much of the original value is preserved. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+mask} & Optional pointer to a mask array; if provided, advection is applied only where the mask is nonzero.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A new \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} representing the advected version of {\ttfamily advected\+\_\+field}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
